***swatch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a> (67226)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> earlier <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language_in_northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:English language in northern England"><a href = vnd.unilang:northern.html>Northern</a> England</a> dialectal <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swache</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> counterfoil <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> counterstock <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tally.html>tally</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1512); <a href = vnd.unilang:further.html>further</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:unknown.html>unknown</a>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">swach</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swath</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">swathe</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">swæcc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:taste.html>taste</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:flavour.html>flavour</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:odour.html>odour</a>; fragrance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:swatch.html>swatch</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular <a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">swatches</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:present.html>present</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">swatching</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:simple.html>simple</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:past.html>past</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:participle.html>participle</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">swatched</b>)
